          src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/vtt/49632993/Shadow_and_Bone__Season_2___Official_Trailer___Netflix.mp4.vtt',
          width: 160,
          height: 90
        }
      ],
      overlay: {
        title: 'Тень и кость',
        description: 'Сезон 2: Трейлер (англ.)',
        embedURL: "https://jumper.film.ru/trailer/2414214",
        onClose: function () {
          cont.style = "";
          const plr = this.player();
          if (plr.isInPiP()) {
            plr.exitPictureInPicture();
          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>

<script>
  function selectContainer2395347() {
    const cont = document.getElementById("trailerCont2395347");
    const videoEl = document.createElement("video");
    videoEl.id = "trailerplayer";
    videoEl.className = "video-js vjs-filmru";
    videoEl.setAttribute("playsinline", "true");
    cont.appendChild(videoEl);
    const player = frPlayer("trailerplayer", {
      autoplay: true,
      preload: 'none',
      poster: '/sites/default/files/styles/thumb_1024x450/public/filefield_paths/forma.jpeg',
      trailer: true,
      sources: [{
        src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/trailers/21119130/A-Silent-Voice-Trailer-rus-2.mp4',
        type: 'video/mp4'
      }],
      thumbnails: [
        {
          src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/vtt/21119130/A-Silent-Voice-Trailer-rus-2.mp4.vtt',
          width: 160,
          height: 90
        }
      ],
      overlay: {
        title: 'Форма голоса',
        description: 'Трейлер #2 (рус.)',
        embedURL: "https://jumper.film.ru/trailer/2395347",
        onClose: function () {
          cont.style = "";
          const plr = this.player();
          if (plr.isInPiP()) {
            plr.exitPictureInPicture();
          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>
<!--/noindex-->

<script>
  function selectContainer2368943() {
    const cont = document.getElementById("trailerCont2368943");
    const videoEl = document.createElement("video");
    videoEl.id = "trailerplayer";
    videoEl.className = "video-js vjs-filmru";
    videoEl.setAttribute("playsinline", "true");
    cont.appendChild(videoEl);
    const player = frPlayer("trailerplayer", {
      autoplay: true,
      preload: 'none',
      poster: '/sites/default/files/styles/thumb_1024x450/public/trailers_frame/ernest_celestine.jpg',
      trailer: true,
      sources: [{
        src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/trailers/50392292/ESNP-09-02.mp4',
        type: 'video/mp4'
      }],
      thumbnails: [
        {
          src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/vtt/50392292/ESNP-09-02.mp4.vtt',
          width: 160,
          height: 90
        }
      ],
      overlay: {
        title: 'Эрнест и Селестина: Новые приключения',
        description: 'Трейлер (рус.)',
        embedURL: "https://jumper.film.ru/trailer/2368943",
        onClose: function () {
          cont.style = "";
          const plr = this.player();
          if (plr.isInPiP()) {
            plr.exitPictureInPicture();
          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>
<!--/noindex-->

<script>
  function selectContainer2378549() {
    const cont = document.getElementById("trailerCont2378549");
    const videoEl = document.createElement("video");
    videoEl.id = "trailerplayer";
    videoEl.className = "video-js vjs-filmru";
    videoEl.setAttribute("playsinline", "true");
    cont.appendChild(videoEl);
    const player = frPlayer("trailerplayer", {
      autoplay: true,
      preload: 'none',
      poster: '/sites/default/files/styles/thumb_1024x450/public/filefield_paths/50426766-2341743.jpeg',
      trailer: true,
      sources: [{
        src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/trailers/50426766/LA-GUERRE-DES-LULUS-rus.mp4',
        type: 'video/mp4'
      }],
      thumbnails: [
        {
          src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/vtt/50426766/LA-GUERRE-DES-LULUS-rus.mp4.vtt',
          width: 160,
          height: 90
        }
      ],
      overlay: {
        title: 'Братство четырех «Л»',
        description: 'Трейлер (рус.)',
        embedURL: "https://jumper.film.ru/trailer/2378549",
        onClose: function () {
          cont.style = "";
          const plr = this.player();
          if (plr.isInPiP()) {
            plr.exitPictureInPicture();
          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>

            plr.exitPictureInPicture();
          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>

      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });

          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;

      poster: '/sites/default/files/styles/thumb_1024x450/public/trailers_frame/marlowe2.jpg',
      trailer: true,
      sources: [{
        src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/trailers/50297814/Marlowe-trailer-rus.mp4',
        type: 'video/mp4'
      }],
      thumbnails: [
        {
          src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/vtt/50297814/Marlowe-trailer-rus.mp4.vtt',
          width: 160,
          height: 90
        }
      ],
      overlay: {
        title: 'Марлоу',
        description: 'Трейлер (рус.)',
        embedURL: "https://jumper.film.ru/trailer/2388727",
        onClose: function () {
          cont.style = "";
          const plr = this.player();
          if (plr.isInPiP()) {
            plr.exitPictureInPicture();
          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>

              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>

            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }

      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }

<script>
  function selectContainer2398671() {
    const cont = document.getElementById("trailerCont2398671");
    const videoEl = document.createElement("video");
    videoEl.id = "trailerplayer";
    videoEl.className = "video-js vjs-filmru";
    videoEl.setAttribute("playsinline", "true");
    cont.appendChild(videoEl);
    const player = frPlayer("trailerplayer", {
      autoplay: true,
      preload: 'none',
      poster: '/sites/default/files/styles/thumb_1024x450/public/trailers_frame/50430909-2398626.jpg',
      trailer: true,
      sources: [{
        src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/trailers/50430909/poehavshaya.mp4',
        type: 'video/mp4'
      }],
      thumbnails: [
        {
          src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/vtt/50430909/poehavshaya.mp4.vtt',
          width: 160,
          height: 90
        }
      ],
      overlay: {
        title: 'Поехавшая',
        description: 'Трейлер (рус.)',
        embedURL: "https://jumper.film.ru/trailer/2398671",
        onClose: function () {
          cont.style = "";
          const plr = this.player();
          if (plr.isInPiP()) {
            plr.exitPictureInPicture();
          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>
<!--/noindex-->

<script>

          cont.style = "";
          const plr = this.player();
          if (plr.isInPiP()) {
            plr.exitPictureInPicture();
          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>
<!--/noindex-->

    </div>

  </div>

<script>
  function selectContainer2414247() {
    const cont = document.getElementById("trailerCont2414247");
    const videoEl = document.createElement("video");
    videoEl.id = "trailerplayer";
    videoEl.className = "video-js vjs-filmru";
    videoEl.setAttribute("playsinline", "true");
    cont.appendChild(videoEl);
    const player = frPlayer("trailerplayer", {
      autoplay: true,
      preload: 'none',
      poster: '/sites/default/files/styles/thumb_1024x450/public/trailers_frame/the-company-you-keep-season-1-trailer-1.jpg',
      trailer: true,
      sources: [{
        src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/trailers/50464731/the-company-you-keep-season-1-trailer-1.mp4',
        type: 'video/mp4'
      }],
      thumbnails: [
        {
          src: 'https://www.film.ru/sites/default/files/vtt/50464731/the-company-you-keep-season-1-trailer-1.mp4.vtt',
          width: 160,
          height: 90
        }
      ],
      overlay: {
        title: 'Твоя компания',
        description: 'Сезон 1: Трейлер (англ.)',
        embedURL: "https://jumper.film.ru/trailer/2414247",
        onClose: function () {
          cont.style = "";
          const plr = this.player();
          if (plr.isInPiP()) {
            plr.exitPictureInPicture();
          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>

      ],

        title: 'Актрисы',
        description: 'Сезон 1: Тизер (рус.)',
        embedURL: "https://jumper.film.ru/trailer/2412327",
        onClose: function () {
          cont.style = "";
          const plr = this.player();
          if (plr.isInPiP()) {
            plr.exitPictureInPicture();
          }
          plr.dispose();
          delete window.trailerPlayer;
        }
      },
      ads: {
        preroll: {
          partnerId: 740822,
          category: 0,
          impId: 2,
          adFoxParameters: {
            ownerId: '301551',
            params: {
              pp: 'g',
              ps: 'dycl',
              p2: 'gtci',
              'target-ref': window.location.href.toString()
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    player.crossorigin('anonymous');
    window.trailerPlayer = player;
    player.on("ready", function () {
      const player = this;
      const makeFS = function () {
        cont.style = "display: block;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.addClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
        else {
          pStyle.width = "90%";
          pStyle.height = "90%";
          pStyle["margin"] = "5vh 5%";
          cont.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
            if (event.target == cont) {
              cont.style = "";
              player.dispose();
              delete window.trailer;
            }
          })
        }
      }
      const makePR = function () {
        const size = Math.max(
            Math.min(window.innerHeight, 526),
            Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) * 0.5622
        );
        cont.style = "display: block; position: relative; height: " + size + "px;";
        player.el().style = "";
        const pStyle = player.el().style;
        pStyle.height = size + "px";
        pStyle["padding-top"] = pStyle.height;
        if (player.mobileMode()) {
          player.removeClass("vjs-fullscreen-pseudo");
        }
      }
      makeFS();
      player.on("widescreenchange", function () {
        if (player.isScreenWide()) {
          makePR();
        }
        else {
          makeFS();
        }
      });
    });
    return player;
  }
</script>
<!--/noindex-->


                    <!--/noindex-->
                                    </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

                      $(window).bind('scroll', function () {
                var load_more_but = $("#load_more");
                if (load_more_but.length && !load_more_but.hasClass('progress-disabled')) {
                    load_more_height = load_more_but[0].offsetTop;
                    scroll_top = $(document).scrollTop();
                    wind_height = window.innerHeight;
                    if (load_more_height < scroll_top + wind_height) {
                        $("#load_more").click();
                        $("#load_more").on('click', function (e) {
                            if ($(this).hasClass('progress-disabled')) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                return false;
                            }
                        });
                    }
                }

                Drupal.behaviors.get_ajax = {
            attach: function (context, settings) {
                jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
                    $('.get-ajax:not(.ajax-processed)').addClass('ajax-processed').each(function () {
                        var element_settings = {};
                        element_settings.progress = {'type': 'throbber'};
                        if ($(this).attr('href')) {
                            element_settings.url = $(this).attr('href');
                            element_settings.event = 'click';
                        }
                        var base = $(this).attr('id');

                        Drupal.ajax[base] = new Drupal.ajax(base, this, element_settings);
                        Drupal.ajax[base].options.type = "GET";
                        var backup = Drupal.ajax.prototype.beforeSerialize;
                        Drupal.ajax.prototype.beforeSerialize = function (element, options) {
                            if (options.type != "GET") backup.call(this, element, options);
                        }
                    });
                })
            }
        };
        //for confirm before ajax
        Drupal.behaviors.confirm_ajax = {
            attach: function (context, settings) {
                jQuery('.use-ajax-confirm:not(.ajax-processed)').filter('a').once('use-ajax-confirm').on('click', function (event) {
                    var $this = jQuery(this);
                    // Allow to provide confirmation message in
                    // data-use-ajax-confirm-message element attribute.
                    var message = $this.data('use-ajax-confirm-message') || Drupal.t('Are you sure you want to do this?');

                    if (confirm(message)) {
                        // Create ajax event only if action was confirmed.
                        var id = $this.attr('id');
                        // Generate unique id, if the element does not already have one.
                        if (!id || id.trim() == '') {
                            id = 'use-ajax-confirm' + new Date().getTime() + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000);
                            $this.attr('id', id);
                        }

                        Drupal.ajax[id] = new Drupal.ajax(id, this, {
                            // 'nojs' to 'ajax' replacement in path performed by Drupal.ajax().
                            url: $this.attr('href'),
                            event: 'load.use-ajax-confirm'
                        });

                        $this.trigger('load.use-ajax-confirm');
                    }

                    return false;
                });
            }
        };

    var cackle_ajax_init = function(id,channel_id) {
        cackle_widget = [];

            var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(mc, s.nextSibling);
        })();
    };
